CREATE TABLE ESG.EAS_DISC_RATE_STATS (
  APPL_ST_YYMM          VARCHAR2(6)        NOT NULL, 
  DISC_RATE_CALC_TYP    VARCHAR2(100)      NOT NULL, 
  INT_RATE_CD           VARCHAR2(100)      NOT NULL, 
  DEPN_VARIABLE         VARCHAR2(50)       NOT NULL, 
  INDP_VARIABLE         VARCHAR2(50)       NOT NULL, 
  APPL_ED_YYMM          VARCHAR2(6)            NULL, 
  REGR_CONSTANT         NUMBER(15, 10)         NULL, 
  REGR_COEF             NUMBER(15, 10)         NULL, 
  REMARK                VARCHAR2(1000)         NULL, 
  VOL                   NUMBER(8, 6)           NULL, 
  LAST_MODIFIED_BY      VARCHAR2(50)           NULL, 
  LAST_UPDATE_DATE      DATE                   NULL
)
TABLESPACE STSESGDT
PCTFREE    10
PCTUSED    0
INITRANS   1
MAXTRANS   255
STORAGE (
    INITIAL     64K
    NEXT        1M
    MINEXTENTS  1
    MAXEXTENTS  UNLIMITED
)
LOGGING
NOCACHE
MONITORING
NOPARALLEL
;

-- 만든 날짜: 2018-10-29 오후 3:50:20
-- 마지막으로 수정한 날짜: 2018-10-29 오후 4:56:33
-- 상태: VALID
------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
DROP TABLE ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

CREATE TABLE ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD (
  APPL_ST_YYMM        VARCHAR2(6)        NOT NULL, 
  LGD_CALC_TYP_CD     VARCHAR2(20)       NOT NULL, 
  SEG_ID              VARCHAR2(20)       NOT NULL, 
  APPL_ED_YYMM        VARCHAR2(6)            NULL, 
  LGD                 NUMBER(15, 10)         NULL, 
  VOL                 NUMBER(8, 6)           NULL, 
  LAST_MODIFIED_BY    VARCHAR2(50)           NULL, 
  LAST_UPDATE_DATE    DATE                   NULL
)
TABLESPACE STSESGDT
PCTFREE    10
PCTUSED    0
INITRANS   1
MAXTRANS   255
STORAGE (
    INITIAL     64K
    NEXT        1M
    MINEXTENTS  1
    MAXEXTENTS  UNLIMITED
)
LOGGING
NOCACHE
MONITORING
NOPARALLEL
;

COMMENT ON TABLE ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD IS '세그먼트 손실률(사용자입력)';

COMMENT ON COLUMN ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD.APPL_ST_YYMM IS '적용 시작 년월';

COMMENT ON COLUMN ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD.LGD_CALC_TYP_CD IS '손실률 산출 유형 코드';

COMMENT ON COLUMN ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD.SEG_ID IS '세그먼트 ID';

COMMENT ON COLUMN ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD.APPL_ED_YYMM IS '적용 종료 년월';

COMMENT ON COLUMN ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD.LGD IS '손실률';

COMMENT ON COLUMN ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD.VOL IS '변동성';

COMMENT ON COLUMN ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD.LAST_UPDATE_DATE IS '최종수정일자';

ALTER TABLE ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD ADD
(
    PRIMARY KEY ( APPL_ST_YYMM, LGD_CALC_TYP_CD, SEG_ID )
        USING INDEX
        TABLESPACE STSESGDT 
        PCTFREE 10
        INITRANS 2
        MAXTRANS 255
        STORAGE (
            INITIAL 64K
            NEXT 1M
            MINEXTENTS 1
            MAXEXTENTS UNLIMITED
        )
);

CREATE PUBLIC SYNONYM EAS_USER_SEG_LGD FOR ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD;

GRANT SELECT ON ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD TO BAS_IF_ROLE;

GRANT SELECT ON ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD TO ESG_RO_ROLE;

GRANT INSERT ON ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD TO ESG_RW_ROLE;

GRANT UPDATE ON ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD TO ESG_RW_ROLE;

GRANT SELECT ON ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD TO ESG_RW_ROLE;

GRANT DELETE ON ESG.EAS_USER_SEG_LGD TO ESG_RW_ROLE;
